  MIN(?a, ?b) = MIN(?b, ?a)
  MUL(?a, ?b) = MUL(?b, ?a)
  OR(?y, ?x) = OR(?x, ?y)
  PLUS(?a, ?b) = PLUS(?b, ?a)
  NE(?y_1, ?x_1) = NE(?x_1, ?y_1)
  MAX(?b, ?a) = MAX(?a, ?b)
  PLUS(?b_1, PLUS(?a, ?b)) = PLUS(?a, PLUS(?b, ?b_1))
  PLUS(?a, PLUS(?b, ?c)) = PLUS(?c, PLUS(?a, ?b)) }
